ELEM 4    2    1    2023 4    5                   The Vision for ZinfiniTree is to maintain and continuously enhance a server design that is both useful and elegant. ELEM 4    1    1    1003 4    1                   -
ELEM 4    1    1    1003 4    3                   ZinFiniTree Client Application Overview
TYPE 4    1    1    1003 4    1    4    1               
ELEM 4    2    1    2007 4    4                   Document Root Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2007 4    5                   Overview
TYPE 4    2    1    2007 4    2    4    1 
ELEM 4    2    1    2008 4    4                   Introduction Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2008 4    5                   Introduction
TYPE 4    2    1    2008 4    2    4    1 
ELEM 4    2    1    2009 4    4                   Introduction P1
ELEM 4    2    1    2009 4    5                   A ZinfiniTree Client Application is a program that sits outside of a ZinfiniTree Server and passes messages to the server and receives responses from the server to perform some useful task.  The Client Application may also have objects defined on the server that support the application.
LINK 4    1    1    1003 4    1    4    2    1    2007                          5179248000.000           
LINK 4    2    1    2007 4    2    4    2    1    2008                          5179248000.000
LINK 4    2    1    2007 4    2    4    2    1    2011                          5179248000.000            
LINK 4    2    1    2008 4    2    4    2    1    2009                          5179248000.000
LINK 4    2    1    2008 4    2    4    2    1    2010                          5179248000.000
LINK 4    2    1    2008 4    2    4    2    1    2028                          5179248000.000
LINK 4    2    1    2011 4    2    4    2    1    2012                          5179248000.000
LINK 4    2    1    2011 4    2    4    2    1    2013                          5179248000.000
ELEM 4    2    1    2010 4    4                   Introduction P2
ELEM 4    2    1    2010 4    5                   ZinfiniTree Client Applications can be categorized as Core and non-Core.  Core applications are of generalized usefulness, providing components that allow development of other applications with minimal or no coding.  Core applications include, Generic Object Maintenance, Document, Spreadsheet, Application Builder and Workflow.  In addition, there are some general-purpose tools that allow for File Import, Object Query and Database Administration.
ELEM 4    2    1    2028 4    4                   Introduction P3
ELEM 4    2    1    2028 4    5                   The applications shown here can be viewed as rough sketches to illustrate possible applications using the ZinfiniTree design approach.  They are also intended to be used as examples of how applications could be built.  The code included can be enhanced or replaced as needed.

ELEM 4    2    1    2011 4    4                   Development Process Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2011 4    5                   Development Process
TYPE 4    2    1    2011 4    2    4    1
ELEM 4    2    1    2012 4    4                   Development Process P1
ELEM 4    2    1    2012 4    5                   The development process begins by thinking about the problem domain and determining the relevant Object Kinds and Object Templates to access the data required.  Then design and assign the Object Elements, Link Types and Type Definitions to the Templates.  This may take some time because it is not always clear where the data should reside.  For example, with an address application should the county be stored with the Address or should there be a separate Object Kind for country and have the Address refer to the country using a Type Definition.  The data design also includes determining what namespaces the new object will be created under.
ELEM 4    2    1    2013 4    4                   Development Process P2
ELEM 4    2    1    2013 4    5                   After the data design is complete, it is time to think about what types of client programs will be needed.  For example, will it be sufficient to maintain your data using Generic Object Maintenance and reporting through standard Spreadsheets or will a custom program be required.  Generic Object Maintenance can be used to maintain data for any object, but it may not be suitable for users in some cases.  For example the Spreadsheet application has a Spreadsheet object that is linked to Columns and Rows.  These linkages can be shown in Generic Object Maintenance but the user will probably be more comfortable looking at an arrangment where Columns or displayed left to right with descriptions accross the top and Rows shown top to bottom with discriptions on the left.

   library--client application--core apps--generic object maintenance
ELEM 4    1    1    1004 4    1                   -
ELEM 4    1    1    1004 4    3                   ZinfiniTree
TYPE 4    1    1    1004 4    1    4    1               
ELEM 4    2    1    2014 4    4                   Generic Object Maintenance Root Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2014 4    5                   Generic Object Maintenance
TYPE 4    2    1    2014 4    2    4    1 
ELEM 4    2    1    2015 4    4                   Generic Object Maintenance The Vision Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2015 4    5                   Vision
TYPE 4    2    1    2015 4    2    4    1 
ELEM 4    2    1    2016 4    4                   Generic Object Maintenance The Vision P1
ELEM 4    2    1    2016 4    5                   The Vision for Generic Object Maintenance is a program that allows any object to be maintained according to the attributes specified by its Template.  The attributes include Object Elements, Type Values and Links.  In addition to the attributes of the primary object being maintained, the program should allow navigation to the objects the primary object is linked to and be able to maintain the attributes of these linked objects using the Object Template that is relevant for the linked object.
ELEM 4    2    1    2024 4    4                   Generic Object Maintenance The Vision P2
ELEM 4    2    1    2024 4    5                   The program should allow for a variety of layouts for maintaining data including, for example, a layout that allows linked objects can be maintained as row formated data.  It should be possible to create new linked objects as needed.  It should be possible to select Type Values from a drop-down based on the Object Set associated with the related Type Definition.  Type Values that are dates should invoke a date selector.  The program should allow for a variety of colors, fonts and sizes of text.

ELEM 4    2    1    2017 4    4                   Generic Object Maintenance--Objects with Namespaces Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2017 4    5                   Objects
TYPE 4    2    1    2017 4    2    4    1 
ELEM 4    2    1    2021 4    4                   Generic Object Maintenance Objects with Namespaces P1
ELEM 4    2    1    2021 4    5                   The Generic Object Maintenance application relies on Object Kinds and Object Templates that are configured in the standard manner.  The Object Template uses Object Kind as a type value and is linked to one or more Technical Profiles which are in turn linked to the relevant Object Elements, Type Definitions and Link Types.  Once configuration is complete, an object can be maintained using Generic Object Maintenance without any specialized coding.

ELEM 4    2    1    2025 4    5                   Code for Generic Object Maintenance can be found in the following code files:  zt_maintain_object.html, zt_client, zt_server and zt_session.

                                                     browser displays web page at http://localhost:3000/zt/ds2_maintain_object  code: in zt_maintain_object.html
                                                     browser calls client at http://localhost:3000/zt/client/maintain_object  code: zt_client.js
                                                       client program interprets the call and extracts the identifiers for the template and the object
                                                       identifiers are used to assemble a query message to the server for the template and object                                                       
                                                       client calls server at http://"+sess1.serverIP+":5001/zt/process_message";   code: zt_server.js
                                                       server returns result of query to the client
                                                       client creates a session using the query response and generates html to maintain the object and returns it to browser which displays it in a new window
                                                       when user clicks submit browser calls /zt/client/maintain_object_submit'
ELEM 4    2    1    2020 4    4                   Generic Object Maintenance--Operating Instructions Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2020 4    5                   Operating Instructions
TYPE 4    2    1    2020 4    2    4    1
ELEM 4    2    1    2027 4    4                   Operating Instructions P1
ELEM 4    2    1    2027 4    5                   Generic Object Maintenance can be invoked by web page server:port/zt_maintain_object or as an App menu option.  In either case the triggering program specifies the namespace of the target ZT Instance, the Language, Status (active or inactive), Maintenance Mode (Create, Change or Display), the Format (Default or Generic), the Namespace and Code of the Template and the Namespace and Code of the Object to be maintained.  After specifying these and clicking Submit, Generic Object Maintenance returns an Object Maintenance screen in a new window.
ELEM 4    2    1    2029 4    4                   Operating Instructions P2
ELEM 4    2    1    2029 4    5                   The Object Maintenance screen displays an object with blank values in Create Mode otherwise the current values of the object are displayed.

ELEM 4    2    1    2035 4    4                   Spreadsheet Vision Heading
ELEM 4    2    1    2035 4    5                   Vision
TYPE 4    2    1    2035 4    2    4    1
ELEM 4    2    1    2039 4    4                   Spreadsheet The Vision P1
ELEM 4    2    1    2039 4    5                   The Vision for the Spreadsheet application is to provide many of the features of a conventional spreadsheet and at the same time take advantage of the data in objects on the ZT Server.  That is to access the Object Elements of individual objects and also to generate rows or columns based on a set of objects.  A Spreadsheet should also be able to display a multi-dimensional set of statistical values. 
ELEM 4    2    1    2042 4    4                   Spreadsheet The Vision P2
ELEM 4    2    1    2042 4    5                   The Spreadsheet application should provide variety of formatting options including setting fonts, text sizes, colors and images.  It should allow refering to URLs that a user can click on an navigate to.  The Spreadsheet should have the capability to refer to a subset of the data in a spreadsheet and export it to a conventional spreadsheet or database.  The Spreadsheet should also contain any other features needed to serve along with Document as the primary reporting applications.
